        <div class="medium-6 cell">
                            <div class="guide-image">

        <div class="medium-6 cell">
            <div class="guide-content">
                <h3 class="guide-name">Acanthoceras zachariasii  </h3>
                <p class="guide-author">(Brun) Simonsen 1979</p>
                <ol class="simple guide-points">
                                                                                            <li>Frustules lightly silicified</li>
                                                                                                <li>Valves with long extensions</li>
                                                                                                <li>Girdle bands numerous</li>
                                                                                                <li>Resting spores distinct</li>
                                                            </ol>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="guide-description">
        Frustules are lightly silicified and typically lie in girdle view. Valves have two long horn-like extensions. Girdle bands are numerous. Resting spores are distinct, and resistant to processing, while the delicate frustules are easily destroyed.
    </div></div></li> </ul><ul data-morphology="monoraphid" class="taxa-species grid-item"><li><h2><a href="https://diatoms.org/genera/achnanthes">Achnanthes</a></h2></li> <li><a href="https://diatoms.org/genera/haslea">Haslea</a></h2></li>  </ul><ul data-morphology="symmetric_biraphid" class="taxa-species grid-item"><li><h2><a href="https://diatoms.org/genera/hippodonta">Hippodonta</a></h2></li> <li><a data-toggle="species-guide-45925" data-dynamic-hover-identifier="species-guide-45925" href="https://diatoms.org/species/hippodonta_capitata" class="species-hover-card-trigger" aria-controls="species-guide-45925" data-is-focus="false" data-yeti-box="species-guide-45925" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">H. capitata  </a> <div id="species-guide-45925" data-dropdown="" data-hover="true" data-hover-pane="true" data-dynamic-endpoint="/dynamic/species/card/45925" data-dynamic-empty-html="false" class="dropdown-guide species-guide dropdown-pane bottom" aria-hidden="true" data-yeti-box="species-guide-45925" data-resize="species-guide-45925" aria-labelledby="1v1snw-dd-anchor" data-e="l4hi75-e"></div></li><li><a data-toggle="species-guide-46518" data-dynamic-hover-identifier="species-guide-46518" href="https://diatoms.org/species/hippodonta_capitata_subsp._iberoamericana" class="species-hover-card-trigger" aria-controls="species-guide-46518" data-is-focus="false" data-yeti-box="species-guide-46518" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">H. capitata subsp. iberoamericana </a> <div id="species-guide-46518" data-dropdown="" data-hover="true" data-hover-pane="true" data-dynamic-endpoint="/dynamic/species/card/46518" data-dynamic-empty-html="false" class="dropdown-guide species-guide dropdown-pane bottom" aria-hidden="true" data-yeti-box="species-guide-46518" data-resize="species-guide-46518" aria-labelledby="rti4fc-dd-anchor" data-e="x4zzwi-e" style="top: 717.7px; left: -71.2667px;"><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x">
        <div class="medium-6 cell">
                            <div class="guide-image">
                    <img src="https://diatoms.org/images/species_guide_images/_square600/Hippodonta_capitata_ssp_ibero_guide.jpg" alt="Hippodonta Capitata Ssp Ibero Guide">
                </div>
                    </div>
        <div class="medium-6 cell">
            <div class="guide-content">
                <h3 class="guide-name">Hippodonta capitata subsp. iberoamericana </h3>
                <p class="guide-author">Metzeltin, Lange-Bert. and García-Rodríguez 2005</p>
                <ol class="simple guide-points">
                                                                                            <li>Valves 4.5-5.4 μm wide</li>
                                                                                                <li>Apices slightly drawn-out</li>
                                                                                                <li>Striae biseriate, 10-11 in 10 μm</li>
                                                            </ol>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="guide-description">
        Valves are rhombic-lanceolate with slightly drawn-out apices. The striae are biseriate and number 10-11 in 10 μm. A hyaline area and one apical row of areolae are present at each end of the valve.
    </div></div></li><li><a data-toggle="species-guide-46171" data-dynamic-hover-identifier="species-guide-46171" href="https://diatoms.org/species/hippodonta_coxiae" class="species-hover-card-trigger" aria-controls="species-guide-46171" data-is-focus="false" data-yeti-box="species-guide-46171" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">H. coxiae  </a> <div id="species-guide-46171" data-dropdown="" data-hover="true" data-hover-pane="true" data-dynamic-endpoint="/dynamic/species/card/46171" data-dynamic-empty-html="false" class="dropdown-guide species-guide dropdown-pane bottom" aria-hidden="true" data-yeti-box="species-guide-46171" data-resize="species-guide-46171" aria-labelledby="n8a6kb-dd-anchor" data-e="o7ehf4-e"></div></li><li><a data-toggle="species-guide-49208" data-dynamic-hover-identifier="species-guide-49208" href="https://diatoms.org/species/hippodonta_gravistriata" class="species-hover-card-trigger" aria-controls="species-guide-49208" data-is-focus="false" data-yeti-box="species-guide-49208" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">H. gravistriata  </a> <div id="species-guide-49208" data-dropdown="" data-hover="true" data-hover-pane="true" data-dynamic-endpoint="/dynamic/species/card/49208" data-dynamic-empty-html="false" class="dropdown-guide species-guide dropdown-pane bottom" aria-hidden="true" data-yeti-box="species-guide-49208" data-resize="species-guide-49208" aria-labelledby="9hp62y-dd-anchor" data-e="90qr8s-e"><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x">
        <div class="medium-6 cell">
                            <div class="guide-image">
                    <img src="https://diatoms.org/images/species_guide_images/_square600/Hippodonta_gravistriata_guide.jpg" alt="Hippodonta Gravistriata Guide">
                </div>
                    </div>
        <div class="medium-6 cell">
            <div class="guide-content">
                <h3 class="guide-name">Hippodonta gravistriata  </h3>
                <p class="guide-author">(Patrick) Potapova 2013</p>
                <ol class="simple guide-points">
                                                                                            <li>Apicies attenuate</li>
                                                                                                <li>Central area transverse, rectangular</li>
                                                                                                <li>Striae uniseriate</li>
                                                            </ol>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="guide-description">
        Valves are rhombic-lanceolate with attenuate apices. The striae are uniseriate, slightly radiate in the center and almost parallel or slightly convergent at the ends. The central area is transverse and rectangular. The raphe is filiform and has tear-drop shaped distal and proximal ends.
    </div></div></li><li><a data-toggle="species-guide-45985" data-dynamic-hover-identifier="species-guide-45985" href="https://diatoms.org/species/hippodonta_hungarica" class="species-hover-card-trigger" aria-controls="species-guide-45985" data-is-focus="false" data-yeti-box="species-guide-45985" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">H. hungarica  </a> <div id="species-guide-45985" data-dropdown="" data-hover="true" data-hover-pane="true" data-dynamic-endpoint="/dynamic/species/card/45985" data-dynamic-empty-html="false" class="dropdown-guide species-guide dropdown-pane bottom" aria-hidden="true" data-yeti-box="species-guide-45985" data-resize="species-guide-45985" aria-labelledby="fgkini-dd-anchor" data-e="10i9th-e"><div class="grid-x grid-margin-x">
        <div class="medium-6 cell">
                            <div class="guide-image">
                    <img src="https://diatoms.org/images/species_guide_images/_square600/Hippodonta_hungarica_guide.jpg" alt="Hippodonta Hungarica Guide">
                </div>
                    </div>
        <div class="medium-6 cell">
            <div class="guide-content">
                <h3 class="guide-name">Hippodonta hungarica  </h3>
                <p class="guide-author">(Grunow) Lange-Bert., Metzeltin and Witkowski 1996</p>
                <ol class="simple guide-points">
                                                                                            <li>Valves 4.2-6.5 μm wide</li>
                                                                                                <li>Valves elliptical-lanceolate with rounded apices</li>
                                                                                                <li>Striae biseriate, 8-11 in 10 μm</li>
                                                            </ol>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="guide-description">
        Valves are elliptical-lanceolate with rounded apices. The striae are biseriate and number 8-11 in 10 μm. A hyaline area and one or two apical rows of areolae are present at each end of the valve.
    </div></div></li><li><a data-toggle="species-guide-51128" data-dynamic-hover-identifier="species-guide-51128" href="https://diatoms.org/species/hippodonta_pseudacceptata" class="species-hover-card-trigger" aria-controls="species-guide-51128" data-is-focus="false" data-yeti-box="species-guide-51128" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false">H. pseudacceptata  </a> <div id="species-guide-51128" data-dropdown="" data-hover="true" data-hover-pane="true" data-dynamic-endpoint="/dynamic/species/card/51128" data-dynamic-empty-html="false" class="dropdown-guide
